<p>159b.5</p>gshegs te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi gdugs tshod gsol nas/ khyim bdag de la chos bstan par brtsams so/ /de dge slong des rgan zhugs de khrid de/ sbyin bdag gi khyim du song ngo / /sbyin bdag gis de gnyis la zas bstabs nas/ de gnyis kyis kho bo cag zas
<p>159b.6</p>bos zin to zhes spangs pa dang / sbyin bdag gis smras pa/ snoms te bzhud la lhag por mdzod te gsol cig /gnyis kyis byin len byas te dong nas rgyal byed kyi tshal du phyin pa dang / dge slong ni chu 'tshag /rgan zhugs ni lhag bor byed du bcug pa na rgan zhugs kyis rang gi skal ba ni
<p>159b.7</p>lhag bor byas la/ dge slong de'i skal ba de ni lhag por ma byas par byas so zhes de zer bcug nas/ de'i 'og tu khyod kyis lhag bor ma byas pa'i bca' ba dang bza' ba zos kyis ltung ba de shogs shig ces byas pa dang / dge slong des smras pa/ rgan zhugs kho bos ltung ba mi 'chags
<p>160a</p>
<p>160a.1</p>kyis/ 'di ltar khyod nyid ltung ba dang bcas par 'gyur ba gang yin pa de lta bu'i gnas yod par 'gyur ro zhes des dge slong rnams la skabs de brjod pa na/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag shes bzhin du dge slong zas zos zin cing / spangs pa
<p>160a.2</p>la skabs tshol zhing ji nas kyang dge slong 'di nyes pa 'byung bar bya'o snyam pa de nyid rkyen du byas nas/ tshe dang ldan pa 'di 'tsho zhig /'di zo shig ces lhag por ma byas pa'i bca' ba dang bza' ba dus kyis stobs par byed/ ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed
<p>160a.3</p>pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang shes bzhin du dge slong zas zos zin cing spangs pa la skabs tshol zhing ci nas kyang dge slong 'di nyes pa 'byung bar bya'o snyam pa de nyid rkyen du byas
<p>160a.4</p>nas/ tshe dang ldan pa 'di 'cho shig /'di zo shig ces lhag por ma byas pa'i bca' ba dang bza' ba dus kyis stobs par byed na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni dge slong rgan zhugs/ nyon mongs pa ni nyes rtsom/ nyes pa ni shes bzhin du
<p>160a.5</p>dge slong zas zos zin cing spangs pa la lhag por ma byas pa'i bza' ba dang ltung ba dus kyis stobs pa'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni chos 'di pa'o/ /shes bzhin du zhes bya ba ni de rang nyid kyis rig pa'am/ gzhan dag gis brjod pas so/ /dge slong zhes bya ba ni chos
<p>160a.6</p>'di pa'o/ /zas zos zin cing spangs pa la zhes bya ba ni yongs su rdzogs shing mthar thug par byas pa la'o/ /skabs tshol zhing zhes bya ba ni klan ka tshol zhing ngo / /ci nas kyang dge slong 'di nyes pa 'byung bar bya'o snyam pa zhes bya ba ni ji nas kyang dge slong 'di lung ba dang bcas par byas
<p>160a.7</p>par 'gyur ro snyam pa'o de nyid rkyen du byas nas zhes bya ba ni gzhan ma yin pa'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa 'di 'cho zhig /'di zo shig ces bya ba ni bca' ba dang bza' ba'o/ /lhag por ma byas pa zhes bya ba ni lhag mar ma byas shing ma bor yongs su ma btang ba'i'o/ /bca' ba dang bza' ba zhes bya ba
<p>160b</p>
<p>160b.1</p>ni bca' ba lnga po dang bza' ba lnga po dag go/ /dus kyis stobs na zhes bya ba ni yang yang du stobs na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis shes bzhin du dge slong zas zos zin cing spangs pa la lhag por ma byas pa'i
<p>160b.2</p>zas rung ba dus kyis stobs na/ spangs pa la stobs pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ zas spangs pa nyid dang / lhag por ma byas pa nyid dag las 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong
<p>160b.3</p>zas spangs pa nyid dang / lhag por ma byas pa nyid dang / der 'du shes pa dang / dus su rung ba'i zas dang bstabs pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /spangs pa la stobs pa'i ltung byed de sum cu lnga pa'o// //'dus shing za ba'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ 
<p>160b.4</p>sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na 'od ma'i tshal bya ka lan dka'i gnas na bzhugs so/ /de'i tshe na lhas byin dge slong rab tu mang po dag dang / lhan cig kun dga' ra ba'i nang du 'dus shing zas za nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir/ dge slong dag kun dga' ra ba'i
<p>160b.5</p>nang na 'dus shing za bar byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ 'dus shing za na dus ma gtogs te ltung byed do/ /de la dus ni 'di
<p>160b.6</p>yin te/ na ba dus so/ /las dus so/ /lam dus so/ /grur zhugs pa dus so/ /'dus pa chen po dus so/ /dge sbyong gi zas dus te/ de la de ni dus yin no zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni rgyal po'i khab/ gang zag ni lhas byin 'khor dang bcas pa/ nyon mongs pa ni mi
<p>160b.7</p>mthun pa'i 'dod pa/ nyes pa ni 'dus shing za ba'o/ /de la 'dus shing zhes bya ba ni mi mthun par za na'o/ /dus ma gtogs te zhes bya ba ni dus bzhag ste'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la dus ni 'di yin te/ na ba dus so zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste/ dge slong na ba
<p>161a</p>
<p>161a.1</p>zas gcig gis 'tsho bar mi nus pa'o/ /las dus so zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste/ dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi'am/ mchod rten gyi las tha na phyag dar re lde tsam mam/ dkyil 'khor ba mal tsam byas pa'o/ /lam dus so zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste dge slong dpag tshad
<p>161a.2</p>phyed du song ba'am/ de'i phyed du song ste phyir 'ongs pa'o/ /grur zhugs pa dus so zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste dge slong grur zhugs pa dpag tshad phyed du song pa'am de'i phyed du song ste phyir 'ongs pa'o/ /'dus pa chen po dus so zhes bya ba ni spags pa'o/ /dge sbyong gi zas dus te zhes bya ba ni
<p>161a.3</p>'di las phyi rol pa'i rab tu byung ba dag 'khod pa de yang dge sbyong zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o/ /de la de ni dus yin no zhes bya ba ni/ bslab pa'i gzhi bca' ba mdzad pa de la ni gnang ba dang mthun pa'i chos yin pa'o/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni dge slong na ba ma yin
<p>161a.4</p>pa dang / las ma byas pa dang / lam du ma song ba dang / grur ma zhugs pa so sor nges pa'i zas kyi gnas can dag las gzhan pa dge 'dun du longs pa'i dge slong cig car du za bas mtshams kyi nang du dge 'dun gzhi'i 'dug gnas su za ba las logs shig tu 'dug ste/ dus ston chen po ma yin pa
<p>161a.5</p>dang / dge sbyong gi zas ma yin pa gang yang rung ba cung zad kyis gzhi'i 'dug gnas su za'am/ 'dus shing za ba gang yang rung ba gcig lam bsrul bar der 'du shes pas dus rung ba'i zas zos na 'dus shing za ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ so sor nges
<p>161a.6</p>pa'i zas kyi gnas can dag las gzhan pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun du gyur pa mtshams kyi nang nas gnas pa dag gis zan lhan cig ma yin pa nyid la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag bcus dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong na ba'am/ las
<p>161a.7</p>byas pa'am/ lam du ma song ba'am/ grur zhugs pa ma yin pa nyid dang / so sor nges pa'i zas kyi gnas can dag las gzhan pa nyid dang / dge 'dun du longs pa'i dge slong cig car za ba dang / mtshams kyi nang nyid dang / dge 'dun gzhi'i 'dug gnas su za ba las logs
<p>161b</p>
<p>161b.1</p>shig tu 'dus pa dang / dus ston chen po ma yin pa dang / dge sbyong gi zas ma yin pa dang / zas gang yang rung ba cung zad kyis gzhi'i 'dug gnas su za ba'am 'dus shing za ba gang yang rung ba gcig la ma bsrul ba dang / der 'dus pa dang / dus su rung ba'i zas zos pa'o/ /de
<p>161b.2</p>dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /'dus shing za ba'i ltung byed de sum cu drug pa'o// //dus ma yin par za ba'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/ rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na
<p>161b.3</p>bzhugs so/ /gang gi tshe tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen pos nye ba 'khor la sogs pa sar pa skyes phran gzhon nu bcu bdun sde'i tshogs rab tu phyung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs par byas pa de'i tshe de dag snga dro sham thabs bgos lhung bzed dang chos gos thogs te/ mnyan yod na bsod snyoms
<p>161b.4</p>la zhugs so/ /bud med ni sred pa spyad pa yin pas bud med kyis de dag mthong nas brang brdungs te smras pa/ 'di dag skyes pa na gang dag gis 'di dag skyes ma thag gi lce lan tshwas 'gengs par ma nus pa dang / brla phrag tu khron pa bcug ste 'brang bar ma nus pa de dag gis ci thob/ bcu bdun
<p>161b.5</p>sde dag nyam nga bar gyur nas smras pa/ bdag cag gis zan bcad par gyur pa ni bla'i/ tshig ngan pa rnam pa 'di lta bu dag thos par gyur pa ni mi rung ngo zhes de dag de nyid nas phyir log ste/ zan bcad par byas nas/ de dag gis ji srid du lus las mdangs ma yal ba de srid du dge ba'i
<p>161b.6</p>phyogs la tron byas nas/ gang gi tshe lus las mdangs yal ba de'i tshe na glos phab ste nyal lo/ /grong khyer ba skyed mos tshal ba dga' ba dag /bza' ba dang ltung thub khyer te/ mnyan yod kyi phyi rol rgyal byed kyi tshal du dong nas 'cha' bar byed/ bza' bar byed/ 'thung bar byed pa nas
<p>161b.7</p>bcu bdun sde dag gis de dag mthong nas lto ba la nyug par byed pa na/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag gsol bzhed dam/ 'dod do/ /de dag gis bcu bdun sde dag la bca' ba dang ltung ba byin pa dang / de dag gis longs spyad nas zung bsdebs te 'chag cing kha ton bya bar
<p>162a</p>
<p>162a.1</p>brtsams pa dang / nye dgas de dag kha ton byed pa mthong nas smras pa/ kye ma'o bcu bdun sde dag gis shin tu brtson 'grus brtsams so/ /btsun pa nye dga' bcom ldan 'das kyis bden chos mngon par brjod par byed do/ /sbyin pa po dang / sbyin bdag gis
<p>162a.2</p>len pa po la zas sbyin pa na gnas lnga sbyin par byed de/ tshe sbyin pa dang / kha dog sbyin pa dang / stobs sbyin pa dang / spobs pa sbyin pa dang / brtson 'grus sbyin pa ni bde bar 'gyur ro zhes bka' stsal ba ni legs par gsungs pa yin te/ zos na stobs dang ldan par 'gyur gyi/ ma zos na mi
<p>162a.3</p>'gyur ro/ /khyod kyis zos sam/ zos so/ /khyed dus ma yin par zar rung ngam/ gal te dus su ma rnyed na kho bo cag gis ltogs te 'chi bar bya'am ci zhes zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag dus ma yin par bca' ba dang / bza' ba za bar byed ces smod par
<p>162a.4</p>byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang dus ma yin par bca' ba'am/ bza' ba 'cha' 'am/ za na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad
<p>162a.5</p>de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni bcu bdun sde/ nyon mongs pa ni sbyor mi bzod pa/ nyes pa ni dus ma yin par za ba'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni bcu bdun sde'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /dus ma yin par zhes bya ba ni/ dus ma yin pa gnyis
<p>162a.6</p>te/ skya rengs ma shar ba dang / phyed yol ba'o/ /bca' ba'am bza' ba zhes bya ba ni/ bca' ba lnga po dang / bza' ba lnga po dag go/ /'cha' 'am zan zhes bya ba ni mgul du mid na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge
<p>162a.7</p>slong mi na bas 'dzam bu'i gling la sogs pa gnas gang na bdag nyid gnas pa'i rang gi nyi ma phyed yol phan chad nas phyi de nyin par gyi skya rengs dang po ma shar bar/ shes bzhin du bca' ba dang bza' ba 'chos sam/ zos na dus ma yin par za ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ 
<p>162b</p>
<p>162b.1</p>dus ma yin pa de nyid la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /de la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong min pa dang / dus ma yin pa nyid dang / der 'du shes pa dang / dus su rung ba'i zas dang / zos pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs
<p>162b.2</p>par na smad do/ /dus ma yin par za ba'i ltung byed de sum cu bdun pa'o// //gsog 'jog gi ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /tshe dang ldan pa nag po'i kun du spyod pa
<p>162b.3</p>ni/ grong ngam grong rdal gang na nye bar bsten cing gnas pa na/ de snga dro sham thabs bgos/ lhung bzed dang chos gos thogs te/ grong ngam grong rdal de nyid du lus shin du bsrungs pa dang / dbang po rnams kyi shin du bsdams pa dang / dran pa shin du nye bar gzhag pas bsod snyoms la
<p>162b.4</p>'jug cing / gal te 'bras chan gsher ba rnyed na ni/ lhung bzed kyis len par byed/ gal te 'bras chan skam po rnyed na ni/ lhung bzed kyi snod kyis len par byed de/ de grong ngam grong rdal der bsod snyoms brgyus nas gtsug lag khang du song ste/ 'bras chan gsher ba ni za bar byed/ 
<p>162b.5</p>'bras chan skam po ni bskams nas/ rdza ma so btang ba bkang ste 'jog par byed cing / de rlung ngam/ yul ngan 'byung ba'am/ char pa 'ba' ba'am/ lhags pa byung bar gyur ba na/ 'bras chan skam po chu dron pos spangs te zos nas bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin
<p>162b.6</p>la snyoms par 'jug pa'i bde ba dag nyams su myong bar byed do/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das dge slong gi tshogs kyis yongs su bskor cing / dge slong gi dge 'dun gyis mdun du bdar te/ gtsug lag khang rgyu zhing gshegs pa na/ tshe dang ldan pa nag po'i gtsug lag khang gal ba der gshegs
<p>162b.7</p>so/ /de'i tshe na tshe dang ldan pa nag po'i gtsug lag khang na 'bras chan skam po rab tu mang po dag bting zhing 'dug pa bcom ldan 'das kyis gzigs nas/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la smras pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos rgyas par gsol to/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
<p>163a</p>
<p>163a.1</p>stsal pa/ kun dga' bo dge slong dag gsog 'jog byas pa za'am/ btsun pa 'tshal lo/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang bca' ba dang bza' ba gsog 'jog byas pa 'cha' 'am za na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan
<p>163a.2</p>yod/ gang zag ni tshe dang ldan pa nag po/ /nyon mongs pa ni bag chags ma byang bas so sor ma brtags pa/ nyes pa ni zas gsog 'jog byas pa za ba'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni/ tshe dang ldan pa nag po'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /bca' ba dang bza' ba zhes bya ba ni
<p>163a.3</p>bca' ba lnga po dang / bza' ba lnga po dag go/ /gsog 'jog byas pa zhes bya ba ni/ gsog 'jog byas pa rnam pa gnyis te/ snga dro byin len byas pa phyi dro'i bar du gsog 'jog byas pa dang / phyi dro byin len byas pa thun tshod las yul bar gsog 'jog byas pa'o/ /'cha' 'am za na zhes bya ba
<p>163a.4</p>ni mgul du mid na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis dus su rung ba'i zas bca' ba lnga po dang / bza' ba lnga po dag las gang yang rung ba byin len byas pa ma zhig pa bca' ba'i phyir 'chad pa phyed yol las 'das
<p>163a.5</p>pa gsog 'jog tu gyur pa la der 'du shes pas zos na gsog 'jog gi ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni dus su rung ba'i zas bca' ba lnga dang bza' ba lnga po dag nyid gsog 'jog tu gyur pa de nyid la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag
<p>163a.6</p>bzhis dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te dus su rung ba'i zas bca' ba 'am bza' bar gtogs pa dang gsog 'jog tu gyur pa dang der 'du shes pa dang zos pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /gsog 'jog gi ltung byed de sum cu brgyad pa'o// //so sor thar pa'i
<p>163a.7</p>mdo'i gzhung 'grel/ bam po bcu gnyis pa/ byin len ma byas par za ba'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen po ni thams cad dur khrod pa dang ldan pa
<p>163b</p>
<p>163b.1</p>yin te de'i lhung bzed kyang dur khrod pa yin/ chos gos kyang dur khrod pa yin/ bsod snyoms kyang dur khrod pa yin/ gnas mal yang dur khrod pa yin te gang gi tshe skye bo phal po che la mi ngas byung ba de'i tshe na tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen po tsho ba dang / pags pa dang sha dang / khrag rgyas par
<p>163b.2</p>gyur pa dang / de yang dang yang du grong du bsod snyoms la 'jug par mi byed la gang gi tshe skye bo phal po che la mi ngas ma byung ba de'i tshe na tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen po rid pa dang / nyam chung ba dang / rke ba dang / skam pa dang / lus ma thob par gyur cing / de yang dang yang du bsod snyoms la 'jug
<p>163b.3</p>par byed do/ /sgo bas de mtshan mar bzung nas 'phags pa nag po chen po 'di mi sha za'am snyam zhing thams cad du yang 'phags pa nag po chen po mi sha za'o zhes sgra grags so/ /mnyan yod na bram ze zhig 'dug pa des/ rigs mnyam pa las chung ma blangs nas/ de de dang lhan cig rtse
<p>163b.4</p>bar byed/ dga' bar byed/ dga' mgur spyod par byed do/ /de'i bu mo zhig byung nas bsring zhing bskyed de chen por gyur to/ /dus gzhan zhig na bram ze de dus la bab nas nye du rnams kyis gos sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po dag gis khyogs spyil brgyan nas dur khrod du khyer
<p>163b.5</p>te bsregs shing dong nas/ de'i chung ma dang bu mo gnyis mtha' gcig tu dong ste bsdad pa dang tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen po de'i gdong du lta zhing / sdod pa mthong nas bu mos smras pa/ yum 'phags pa nag po chen po 'di bya rog mo zhar ma bzhin du nges par rtog cing sdod do zhes/ ngag gi las rtsub
<p>163b.6</p>mo yang smras par gyur to/ /mnyan yod na bram ze'i khye'u dag gis/ 'phags pa nag po chen po mi sha za'o zhes thos nas/ de dag gis de bgam pa'i phyir gcig shi ba'i cha lugs su byas nas/ yung ba dang 'bru mar gyis bskus te/ khyogs spyil du bzhag nas mnyan yod nas phyir
<p>163b.7</p>'byung bar brtsams pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen po yang mnyan yod du bsod snyoms la zhugs te/ des de mthong nas bsams pa/ bdag dgang dka' ba 'di'i don du grong du bsod snyoms la zhugs te ci rung / phyir log la zas lnga po 'di dag nyid bza' bar bya'o snyam nas de
<p>164a</p>
<p>164a.1</p>phyir log go/ /de dag gis de dur khrod du bor te/ mtha' gcig tu dong nas tshang tshing dang lhab lhub dag gi nang du mgo dkris te bsdad do/ /der wa zhig gis bgrod par brtsams pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa nag po chen pos bsams pa/ was zas lnga po dag zos
<p>164a.2</p>shing bdag zan chad par gyur na mi rung ngo snyam du rig nas/ des myur ba myur bar 'gro bar brtsams pa dang / bram ze'i khye'u de skrag ste/ kho bo zos so kho bo zos so zhes ngu bar brtsams so/ /bram ze'i khye'u de dag dbyug pa thogs te myur ba myur bar dong nas de dag gis smras pa/ 
<p>164a.3</p>'phags pa drang srong gi rgyal mtshan thogs shing / sdig pa'i las rtsub po 'di dag dang / 'di lta bu dag lhag par spyod dam/ des smras pa ji byas mi sha za'o/ /bzhin bzangs dag ci khyed kyis kho bo mtshon thogs te/ sha gcod cing za ba mthong ngam/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'o na
<p>164a.4</p>ci'i slad du myur ba myur bar byon/ /bzhin bzangs dag /kho bo la blo skyes pa/ wa 'dis zas lnga po 'di dag zos shing bdag gi zan chad par gyur na mi rung ngo snyam du rig nas myur ba myur bar 'ongs so/ /'phags pa zas lnga po dag gsol lam/ mi sha gsol ni ma 'tshal gyi 'di ltar
<p>164a.5</p>thams cad du 'phags pa nag po chen po mi sha gsol zhes ni grags par gyur ro zhes zer ba'i skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/ nyes dmigs gang cung zad cig byung ba de ni dge slong dag byin len byed du ma
<p>164a.6</p>bcug par za bar gyur pa yin pas/ de lta bas na dge slong rnams kyis byin len byed du bcug ste/ za na de nyid dpang por 'gyur ro snyam du dgongs nas bka' stsal pa/ de lta bas na dge slong rnams kyis byin len byed du bcug ste bza' bar bya'o/ /byin len ni rnam pa lnga ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ lus
<p>164a.7</p>kyis lus su dang / lus dang 'brel bas lus su dang / lus kyis lus dang 'brel bar dang / lus dang 'brel pas lus dang 'brel pa dang / gzhag pa'i cho ga dag ni lnga pa'o/ /rung ba ni rnam pa lnga ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ mes rung ba dang / mtshon gyis rung ba dang / sen mos rung ba dang / rnyis
<p>164b</p>
<p>164b.1</p>pas rung ba dang / ne tshos rma byung bas rung ba nyid ni lnga pa'o/ /gzhan yang rung ba rnam pa lnga ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ phyung ba dang / gshegs pa dang / bcad pa dang / phug pa dang / sa bon gyi chos nyid med pa nyid ni lnga ba'o/ /lag pa bkan par byin len rnam pa lnga ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ man shel dang / 
<p>164b.2</p>khri dang / khri'u dang / thu ba dang / lhung bzed bzhi nyid lnga pa'o/ /mes rung bar bya ba ni phung por byas te/ mes gnas pa gnyis sam/ gsum du reg par byas nas thams cad rung bar 'gyur ro/ /mtshon dang sen mos ni re re nas so/ /khyim pa rnams mi snyoms par [(]'drim [,]'brim [)]nas/ dge slong
<p>164b.3</p>rnams kyis dge tshul dag 'drim du gzhug par bya'o/ /de dag kyang mi snyoms na/ dge slong dag gis lag pa bsnyal te/ byin len byas nas brim par bya'o/ /'on kyang ma snyoms na brim par bya ba gces pa dang / bar ma dang / tha ma dag so sor bya'o/ /'drim par byed pa'i skal ba ni/ 
<p>164b.4</p>mkhan po dang slob dpon nam/ drung na 'dug pa de dag gis mnod par bya'o/ /stan nas ma 'phags pas ji tsam zhus pa de tsam dag byin len byed du gzhug go/ /'dril ba dag stan las ma 'phags pas len nus pa dag ni byin len byed du gzhug mi dgos la/ mi nus pa dag ni yang byin
<p>164b.5</p>len byed du gzhug par bya'o/ /khyim pa dag kyang 'drim du gzhug par bya zhing / dge slong gis dang por gzung zhing khyim pas phyis gzung bar bya ba'o/ /dge slong dag las blangs pa gang yin pa de dag gi byin len ni de nyid yin no/ /khyim pa dag las blangs pa gang yin pa de dag ni/ byin
<p>164b.6</p>len byed du gzhug go/ /dang por dge slong dag gis gtang bar bya zhing / phyis khyim pa dag gis gtang bar bya ste/ phyis de nyin par dge 'dun la brim par bya'o/ /bram ze dang khyim bdag dad pa can dge 'dun la zhun mar gyi bum pa la sogs pa dag 'bul na blang par bya zhing / blangs nas dge
<p>164b.7</p>'dun la brim par bya'o/ /de dag gis chos gos dag snum par gyur pa lta na bar du rtswa 'am/ lo ma dag bcug ste brim par bya'o/ /de dag bzung ste 'greng ba na ngal bar 'gyur ba lta na gzhag par bya'o/ /gzhag pa na 'dril ba lta na 'og gzhi la gzhag par bya'o/ /snod phul ba dag
<p>165a</p>
<p>165a.1</p>kyang blangs shing chu'i rdzing bu zab mo'i nang du zhag bdun nam brgyad gzhug par bya zhing / /gang nya'am/ rus sbal lam/ sbal pa'am/ chu srin byis pa gsod pa'am/ nya khyi pa dag gis ma lus par ldags par gyur pa/ de'i tshe rung ba'i khang par bcug ste spyad
<p>165a.2</p>par bya'o/ /rnam pa lngas ni byin len byed du ma bcug par brjod par bya ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ mtshams kyi phyi rol na 'dug pas dang / mi 'thob pa'i phyogs nas dang / glo nas dang / rgyab nas dang / lag pa khas phub pas byin len byed du 'jug pa'o/ /rnam pa lngas ni/ byin len
<p>165a.3</p>byed du bcug par brjod par bya'o/ /lnga gang zhe na/ snga ma las bzlog pa dag gis so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis byin len byed du bcug ste bza' bar bya'o zhes bka' stsal nas/ drug sde dag byin len byed du bcug pa dang / byin len byed du ma bcug pa yang za bar byed nas/ dge slong
<p>165a.4</p>don nyung ngu dag bcom ldan 'das kyis byin len byed du bcug ste bza' bar bya'o zhes bka' stsal na/ ci'i phyir dge slong dag byin len byed du bcug pa dang / byin len byed du ma bcug pa yang za bar byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtang bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams
<p>165a.5</p>kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang ma byin par kha nas mid pa'i zas za na chu dang so shing ma gtogs te ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni drug sde/ nyon mongs pa ni bka' dang bslab
<p>165a.6</p>pa la g.yel ba/ nyes pa ni byin len byed du ma bcug par za ba'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni drug sde'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /ma byin par zhes bya ba ni de la skyes pa'am/ bud med dam/ ma ning gang gis kyang ma byin pa'o/ /kha nas med pa'i zas zhes
<p>165a.7</p>bya ba ni/ bca' ba lnga po dang / bza' ba lnga po dag go/ /za na zhes bya ba ni mgul du mid na'o/ /chu dang so shing ma gtogs te zhes bya ba ni chu dang so shing bzhag ste'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis byang gi sgra mi
<p>165b</p>
<p>165b.1</p>snyan pa'i dus dang / chu dang so shing ma gtogs pa'i bza' bar bya ba byin len ma bstabs pa nyid la 'du shes pas khar zos na byin len ma byas par za ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni byang gi sgra mi snyan pa'i dus dang / chu dang so shing ma gtogs pa'i bza'
<p>165b.2</p>bar bya ba byin len ma bstabs pa nyid la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag drug gis dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa'i dus ma gtogs pa dang / chu dang so shing ma gtogs pa'i bza' bar bya ba dang / byin len gyi mtshan nyid mngon
<p>165b.3</p>sum du mtshams kyi nang du 'thob pa'i phyogs na 'dug pa'am/ lag pa bkan pas lus sam de dang 'brel par gyen du 'brel bar 'dug nus pa/ bsnyen par ma rdzogs pa mi ma yin pa las kyang sbyin par 'dod pas yan lag gis sam/ de dang 'brel bas byin nang mnos pa'i byin
<p>165b.4</p>len ma bstabs pa nyid dang / der 'du shes pa dang / khar bcug pa dang / zos pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /byin len ma byas par za ba'i ltung byed de sum cu dgu pa'o// //bsod pa slong ba'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
<p>165b.5</p>ldan 'das shAkya rnams kyi nang du ljongs rgyu zhing gshegs pa na/ ser skya'i gnas su byon nas/ ser skya'i gnas na n+ya gro d+ha'i kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /shAkya ming chen gyis de thos nas bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis
<p>165b.6</p>la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ mtha' gcig tu 'dug go/ /mtha' gcig tu 'dug nas bcom ldan 'das kyis shAkya ming chen la chos dang ldan pa'i bka' mchid kyis yang dag par ston par mdzad/ yang dag par 'dzin du 'dzud par mdzad/ yang dag par gzengs stod par
<p>165b.7</p>mdzad/ yang dag par rab tu dga' bar mdzad do/ /rnam grangs du mar chos dang ldan pa'i bka' mchid kyis yang dag par bstan/ yang dag par 'dzin du bcug /yang dag par gzengs bstod/ yang dag par rab tu dga' bar mdzad nas cang mi gsung ngo / /de nas shA kya ming chen
<p>166a</p>
<p>166a.1</p>gyis/ bcom ldan 'das dge slong gi dge 'dun dang bcas pa sang bdag gi sdum par/ gdugs tshod gsol bar ci gnang zhes spyan drangs nas gshegs te gdugs tshod gsol nas/ shAkya ming chen la chos bstan nas gdan las bzhengs te gshegs so/ /
<p>166a.2</p>de'i nang par drug sde dag sngar langs te sbyin bdag gi khyim du song ba dang / de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag 'di nyid du gdugs tshod gsol cig /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ kho bo cag mgron du bos so/ /sus/ shAkya ming chen gyis so/ /'o na sang gdugs tshod gsol cig /
<p>166a.3</p>de ltar bya'o zhes drug sde dag gis sbyin bdag de dag phyi de nyin par gyi zan drug cu sbyor du bcug nas/ shAkya ming chen gyi khyim du dong ba dang / ci tsam de na kha zas sta gon byas pa yang med gnas mal bshams pa yang med par mthong nas/ drug sde dag gis/ shAkya ming chen gyi zho shas 'tsho ba dag
<p>166a.4</p>la smras pa/ shes ldan dag /khyed kyis sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun spyan drangs nas/ snying las chung dur 'khod cing gdugs tshod kyang sta gon mi byed/ gnas mal yang shom par mi byed na/ ci sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi gdugs tshod gcod
<p>166a.5</p>par byed dam/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag khyed cag mnal bar gyur tam ci/ sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun gdugs tshod gsol te gshegs lags so/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ ci kho bo cag gi zan gcad par bya'am/ de dag gis smras pa/ 
<p>166a.6</p>'phags pa dag bdag cag gis/ shAkya ming chen la sbran gyi bar du re zhig yud tsam zhig gzhes shig ces de dag dong ste/ shAkya ming chen la smras pa/ 'phags pa drug sde dag da gzod mchis te 'tshal ma slong ngo / /shAkya ming chen gyis smras pa/ deng la lhag rol cung zad cig yod pa de
<p>166a.7</p>byin cig /de dag dong ste smras pa/ 'phags pa dag bzhugs la gsol cig ces de dag gis brim par brtsams pa dang / drug sde dag gis smras pa/ shAkya ming chen gyis kha shin du chen pos/ bcom ldan 'das kyis sang bdag gi sdum par dge slong gi dge 'dun dang thabs cig tu
<p>166b</p>
<p>166b.1</p>gdugs tshod gsol bar ci gnang zhes spyan drang nas/ gal te zan 'di 'dra bas sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun spyan drang du rung na ni/ nye dgas kyang nyi ma re re zhing sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun spyan 'dren par 'gyur ro/ /'di ltar bkren pa 'di la
<p>166b.2</p>ci bdog gis deng la khyim bdag che ge mo'i khyim nas 'o ma long shig che ge mo'i khyim nas zho long shig /che ge mo'i khyim nas mar long shig /che ge mo'i khyim nas nya long shig /che ge mo'i khyim nas sha long shig /che ge mo'i khyim nas sha skam dag long shig ces de dag gis bdag
<p>166b.3</p>nyid kyi phyir/ zas bsod pa de lta bu dag gzhan gyi khyim dag nas blangs te zos nas gtsug lag khang du dong ba dang / dge slong rnams kyis de dag la smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa dag khyed kyis zan gar zos/ de nyid du'o/ /khyed cag de nam mthong ngo / /kho bo cag phyis lhags so/ /khyed
<p>166b.4</p>cag gis zan ji lta bu zos/ 'o ma dang zho dang mar dang / nya dang sha dang sha skam dag zos so/ /dge slong dag gis smras pa/ kho bo cag gis zas de lta bu ma thob bo/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ bkren pa de la zas de lta bu ga la yod/ kho bo cag gis khyim du 'gro ba'i khyim
<p>166b.5</p>dag nas blangs te der zos so/ /khyed cag bdag nyid kyi phyir zas bsod pa de lta bu dag /gzhan gyi khyim dag nas blangs te zar rung ngam/ rung yang srid/ mi rung yang srid de/ kho bo cag gis ltogs te 'chi bar bya'am zhes zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag
<p>166b.6</p>bdag nyid kyi phyir/ zas bsod pa de lta bu dag gzhan gyi khyim dag nas blangs te 'cha' ba dang / za bar byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma
<p>166b.7</p>bzhin du/ bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams kyi zas bsod pa gang dag gsungs pa 'di lta ste/ 'o ma dang zho dang mar dang / nya sha dang / sha dang / sha skam dag ste/ yang dge slong gang mi na bar bdag nyid kyi phyir/ zas bsod pa de lta bu dag gzhan gyi khyim dag nas blangs te
<p>167a</p>
<p>167a.1</p>'cha' 'am za na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni ser skya'i gnas/ gang zag ni drug sde/ nyon mongs pa ni rang nyam dang lto 'dun/ nyes pa ni mi na bar bdag nyid kyi phyir zas bsod pa dag gzhan gyi khyim dag nas blangs te za ba'o/ /de la bcom ldan
<p>167a.2</p>'das kyis zhes bya ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so/ /dge slong rnams kyi zhes bya ba ni/ chos 'di pa rnams kyi'o/ /zas bsod pa gang dag gsungs pa zhes bya ba ni rab tu bstan pa'o/ /'di lta ste/ 'o ma dang / zho dang / mar dang / nya
<p>167a.3</p>sha dang / sha dang / sha skam dag ste zhes bya ba ni/ zas bsod pa dag go/ /dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni drug sde'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /mi na bar zhes bya ba ni na ba ma gtogs par ro/ /bdag nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid la bsngos te'o/ /zas bsod pa de lta bu
<p>167a.4</p>dag ces bya ba ni/ 'o ma dang / zho dang / mar dang / nya sha dang / sha dang / sha skam dag go/ /gzhan gyi khyim dag nas zhes bya ba ni bram ze dang khyim bdag gi khyim dag nas so/ /bslangs te zhes bya ba ni slong mo byas pa'o/ /'cha' 'am za na zhes bya ba ni mgul du mid na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni
<p>167a.5</p>snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong mi na ba ji bder bstabs pa ma byas sam sbyin par byed pa nye du ma yin pa khyim pa nyid las zas bsod pa'o ma'am/ zho'am/ mar ram/ nya sha'am/ sha'am/ sha skam lta bu rang gis bslangs te zos pa dang / 
<p>167a.6</p>ngan pa'am/ bsod pa'am/ tha mal pa'am/ bzang po thob pa na zas bsod pa snga ma dag lta bu rang gis bslangs te zos na/ bsod pa slong ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ dge slong mi na ba ji bder bstabs pa byam byas pa nyid dang / sbyin par byed pa nye du
<p>167a.7</p>ma yin pa'i khyim pa nyid dang / zas bsod pa dag ni byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong min ba nyid dang / ji bder bstabs pa ma byas pa nyid dang / zas bsod pa nyid dang / sbyin par byed pa nye du ma yin pa khyim bdag nyid
<p>167b</p>
<p>167b.1</p>dang / bslangs te zos pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /bsod pa slong ba'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu pa'o// //sdom la/ srog chags bcas dang nyal sar 'dug /'greng dang gcer bu dmag dang ni/ /zhag gnyis bshams dkrugs 'gro ba dang / /
<p>167b.2</p>rdeg dang gzas dang gnas ngan len/ /zhes bya ba ni bcu pa lnga pa yin te/ sdom la zhes bya ba'i tshig gi don dang / dgos pa ni snga ma bzhin no/ /bcu pa lnga pa 'dis kyang ltung byed kyi chos bcu bstan te/ srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod pa dang / nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim
<p>167b.3</p>na 'dug pa dang / nyal bo byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'greng ba dang / gcer bu la sbyin pa dang / dmag la lta ba dang / dmag gi nang na gnas pa dang / dpung gi yan lag nyams su myong ba dang / rdeg pa dang / gzas pa dang / gnas ngan len 'chab pa'i ltung byed do/ /de la srog
<p>167b.4</p>chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kau shAm+bI na gdangs can gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /tshe dang ldan pa 'dun pa shes bzhin du srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod nas/ de la dge slong rnams kyis smras pa/ tshe dang
<p>167b.5</p>ldan pa 'dun pa khyod shes bzhin du srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la ma spyod cig /des smras pa/ kho bo la 'ga' zhig gis bsgrangs te gtad dam ci/ shar gyi rgya mtsho chen por 'dong na ci nyes/ lho dang / nub dang / byang gi rgya mtsho chen por 'dong na ci nyes/ 'bab chu dang / mtsho dang / 
<p>167b.6</p>lteng ka dag tu 'jug na ci nyes zhes zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag shes bzhin du/ srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol
<p>167b.7</p>to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang shes bzhin du srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod na ltung byed do zhes bca' pa mdzad de/ yul ni kau shAm+bI/ gang zag ni 'dun pa/ nyon mongs pa ni bag med pa/ nyes pa ni shes bzhin du srog chags dang / 
<p>168a</p>
<p>168a.1</p>bcas pa'i chu la spyod pa'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni 'dun pa'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /shes bzhin du zhes bya ba ni de rang nyid kyis rig par gyur pa'am/ gzhan dag gis brjod pas so/ /srog chags dang bcas pa zhes bya ba ni/ 
<p>168a.2</p>srog chags dang bcas pa rnam pa gnyis te/ gang dag mig sngar snang bar gyur pa dang / gang dag chu tshags kyis zin par 'gyur ba'o/ /chu la spyod na zhes bya ba ni/ chu'i spyod pa gnyis su ste/ nang gi dang phyi rol gyi'o/ /nang gir spyod pa ni khrus byed pa dang / 'thung ba dang / so shing 'dor ba
<p>168a.3</p>dang / lag pa dang / rkang pa dag 'khru ba'o/ /phyi rol gyir spyod pa ni/ lhung bzed bkru ba dang / lhung bzed chung ngu bkru ba dang / chos gos dag bkru ba dang / tshon gyi las byed pa dang / gtsug lag khang du chag chag 'debs pa dang / zhal zhal skud pa dang / lci ba sar pa'i byug pas nyug
<p>168a.4</p>pa'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni/ sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas ngan song dang / ngan 'gro dang / log par ltung ba dag tu sreg par byed/ 'tshed par byed/ ltung bar byed pa'o/ /gzhan yang ji srid du ltung ba de ma bshags shing so sor ma bshags na/ 
<p>168a.5</p>dge ba'i chos rnams la sgrib par byed pa ste/ des na ltung byed do zhes gsungs so/ /sngar srog chags dang bcas pa la spyod pa'i ltung byed bstan pa dang / 'dir srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod pa'i ltung byed bstan pa de gnyis kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid ni 'dra'o/ /bye brag tu ni/ snga ma ni
<p>168a.6</p>rang spyod pa ma yin/ gzhan spyod pa'i don nyid la 'jug pa dang / 'jug du 'jud pa de gnyis kyi yul la rnam par gzhag go/ /'di ni rang spyod pa'i don nyid la 'jug pa dang / 'jug tu 'jud pa de gnyis kyi yul la rnam par gzhag go/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par
<p>168a.7</p>gzhag pa ni/ dge slong rang spyod pa'i don du lus kyi nye bar spyod pa'i mtshan nyid dang / de'i ngo bo nyid khrus dang btung ba dang / so shing dor ba dang / lag pa dang rkang pa bkru ba dang / lus kyi yo byad bza' bar bya ba dang / lhung bzed dang / chos gos dang / gnas dang / so bkru ba dang / me la
<p>168b</p>
<p>168b.1</p>sogs pa dang / yo byad de dag tu nye bar sbyar bas dang / lci ba dang / tshon dang / rtswa dang / shing la sogs pa dang / nye bar sbyar ba de dag las chu la sogs pa dgos pa 'di lta ste/ byi dor bya ba dang / bkru ba dang / kha bsgyur ba dang / chag chag gdab pa dang / phyag dar bya ba dang / zhal
<p>168b.2</p>zhal bya ba dang / 'u sha dang / thang dang / thug pa dag tu bya ba'i chu dang / zhun mar dang / 'bru mar dang / sbrang rtsi dang / bu ram gyi dbu ba dang / 'o ma dang / mar dang / tshwa dang / 'bru'i tshwa dang / zho ga chu dang / rtsab mo dang / shing thog dang / bca' bar bya ba la sogs pa/ dud 'gro'i skye
<p>168b.3</p>gnas su skyes pa'i srog chags bltar nus pas snang ba dag gis srog chags dang bcas pa dang / chu'i srol dgag pa dang / bsal ba dag dang / shing dang g.yeng ba dag chur gzhug pa dang / drang ba dang / bshal ba dag dang / gos rim pa gcig pa las gzhan pa spu can la sogs pa
<p>168b.4</p>bkru ba dang / gos rim pa gcig pa de yang srog chags kyi khams lhag par mang ba'i chur 'khru ba lta bu'i sbyor ba dag la yang srog chags dang bcas pa nyid du 'du shes pas rang nyid 'jug gam/ gzhan 'jug tu 'jud na/ dud 'gro'i skye gnas su skyes pa'i srog chags re re shi ba'i mthar/ 
<p>168b.5</p>srog chags dang bcas pa'i chu la spyod pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni rang spyod pa'i don du chu la sogs pa srog chags dang bcas pa la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ rang spyod pa'i don gang
<p>168b.6</p>yang rung ba dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas su gtogs pa'i srog chags gang yang rung ba dang bcas pa'i chu la sogs pa dang / der 'du shes pa dang / rang dang gzhan gyis spyad pa dang / srog chags ji snyed shi ba'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /srog chags dang bcas
<p>168b.7</p>pa'i chu la spyod pa'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu gcig pa'o// //nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'dug pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /tshe dang ldan pa 'char ka
<p>169a</p>
<p>169a.1</p>bsam pa'i nor bu'i rig pa shes te/ de snga dro sham thabs bgos/ lhung bzed dang chos gos thogs te/ mnyan yod du bsod snyoms la zhugs so/ /mnyan yod na spos 'tshong gi khye'u chung ma blangs nas ring po ma lon pa zhig 'dug pa des zong bkram pa na/ bdag
<p>169a.2</p>chung ma dang lhan cig dga' mgur spyod du 'gro'o snyam pa'i tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i yid la byed pa skyes nas/ des zong phyir bsdu bar brtsams pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'char kas de'i bsam pa shes nas/ bdag song la 'di re ba med par bya'o snyam nas/ de dang por de'i khyim du song ste
<p>169a.3</p>stan la 'dug nas/ bu mo de la chos ston par brtsams so/ /ji tsam na spos 'tshong gi khye'u de 'ongs nas/ des chung ma la smras pa/ 'phags pa 'char ka la bsod snyoms phul la bzhud du gsol cig /tshe dang ldan pa 'char kas smras pa/ bzhin bzangs kho bos bdag nyid kyi dge
<p>169a.4</p>ba'i phyogs yongs su nyams par byas te 'ongs nas chos ston par byed na/ khyod chos nyan mi 'dod dam/ 'dug la chos nyon cig ces des de nan gyis 'dug du bcug ste/ des ci tsam gyis de'i kun nas dkris pa dang bral ba de tsam du chos bstan pa dang / de shAkya'i bu'i dge
<p>169a.5</p>sbyong rnams kyi dge sbyong gi tshul ni tshig go/ /bram ze'i tshul ni tshig ste/ 'di ltar rang gi chung ma la yang dbang med do zhes smad par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag shes bzhin du nyal po byed par shom pa'i
<p>169a.6</p>khyim du phyis gnon byas te stan la 'dug par byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du yang dge slong gang shes bzhin du nyal po byed par
<p>169a.7</p>shom pa'i khyim du phyis gnon byas te stan la 'dug na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni 'char ka /nyon mongs pa ni 'dod chags kyi kun du sbyor ba/ nyes pa ni shes bzhin du nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim du phyis gnon byas te stan la 'dug
<p>169b</p>
<p>169b.1</p>pa'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni 'char ka'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /shes bzhin du zhes bya ba ni de rang nyid kyis rig par gyur pa'am/ gzhan dag gis brjod pas so/ /nyal po byed par shom pa'i zhes bya ba ni/ bud med ni skyes pa'i nyal po bya ba yin la/ 
<p>169b.2</p>skyes pa ni bud med la nyal po byed pa yin no/ /khyim du zhes bya ba ni/ bram ze dang khyim bdag gi khyim du'o/ /phyis gnon byas te zhes bya ba ni phyis zhugs te'o/ /stan la zhes bya ba ni gzhi la'o/ /'dug na zhes bya ba ni 'dom gang gi nang du rkub tshos bzhag na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma
<p>169b.3</p>bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong 'jigs pa'i dbang dang gnas gzhan la sems gtod pa ma yin pas/ khyim pa'i skyes pa dang bud med gnas gzhan mthong bas spyod yul gyi mtha' tshun chad kyi gza' tha dad pa ma yin pa nyid dang / mi
<p>169b.4</p>gzhan med pa nyid kyis sprad du rung ba nyid dang / 'khrig pa spyod pa la zhugs pa'am/ phyogs par shes bzhin du mngon sum du brnag pas 'dug na nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'dug pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ khyim pa'i skyes pa dang / bud
<p>169b.5</p>med dge slong rang gi gnas las gzhan nyid dang / mi gzhan med pa nyid kyis sprad du rung ba nyid na/ 'khrig pa spyod pa la zhugs pa'am/ phyogs pa la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag bdun gyis dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong 'jigs
<p>169b.6</p>pa'i dbang dang / gnas gzhan la sems gtod pa ma yin pa nyid dang / khyim pa skyes pa dang bud med nyid dang / gnas gzhan mthong ba'i spyod yul gyi mtha' tshun chad kyi gza' tha dad pa ma yin pa nyid dang / mi gzhan med pa nyid kyis sprod du rung ba nyid dang / 'khrig pa'i spyod
<p>169b.7</p>pa la zhugs pa'am phyogs pa nyid dang / der 'du shes pa nyid dang / mngon sum du brnag pas 'dug pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'dug pa'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu gnyis pa'o// //nyal po byed par
<p>170a</p>
<p>170a.1</p>shom pa'i khyim na 'greng pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /tshe dang ldan pa 'char ka bsam pa'i nor bu'i rig pa shes te/ de snga dro
<p>170a.2</p>sham thabs bgos lhung bzed dang chos gos thogs te/ mnyan yod du bsod snyoms la zhugs so/ /mnyan yod na spos 'tshong gi khye'u chung ma blangs nas ring po ma lon pa zhig 'dug pa des/ zong bkram pa na/ bdag chung ma dang lhan cig dga' mgur spyod du 'gro'o snyam pa'i
<p>170a.3</p>tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa skyes nas/ des zong phyir bsdu bar brtsams pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'char kas de'i bsam pa shes nas/ bdag song la blta'o snyam nas/ de dang por de'i khyim du song ste/ sgo glegs kyi rgyab na mgo bsring zhing 'greng ngo / /de'i 'og tu
<p>170a.4</p>spos 'tshong [(]gyi [,]gi [)]khye'u de 'ongs nas des chung ma khrid de gnas khang du zhugs pa dang / bu mo des/ 'char ka bden pa na 'greng ba mthong nas/ des khyo la smras pa/ rje'i sras 'phags pa 'char ka sgo glegs kyi rgyab na 'greng ngo / /spos 'tshong gi khye'us smras pa/ 'phags pa 'char ka
<p>170a.5</p>gtsug lag khang na bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par 'jug pa'i bde ba dag nyams su myong zhing 'greng ngo zhes des chung ma la dga' mgur spyad nas/ de gang gi tshe kun nas dkris pa dang bral bar gyur pa de'i tshe na/ des 'char ka mthong ba dang
<p>170a.6</p>de shAkya'i bu'i dge sbyong rnams kyi dge sbyong gi tshul ni tshig go/ /bram ze'i tshul ni tshig ste/ 'di ltar rang gi chung ma la yang dbang med do zhes smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir/ dge slong dag shes bzhin du nyal po
<p>170a.7</p>byed par shom pa'i khyim du/ dben pa skyabs yod par 'greng bar byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang
<p>170b</p>
<p>170b.1</p>shes bzhin du nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim du dben pa skyabs yod pa na 'greng na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni 'char ka /nyon mongs pa ni 'dod chags kyi kun du sbyor ba/ nyes pa ni shes bzhin du nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim du dben pa skyabs
<p>170b.2</p>yod par 'greng ba'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni 'char ka'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /shes bzhin du zhes bya ba ni/ de rang nyid kyis rig par gyur pa'am/ gzhan dag gis brjod pas so/ /nyal po byed par shom pa'i zhes bya ba ni/ bud med ni skyes pa'i
<p>170b.3</p>nyal po bya ba yin la/ skyes pa ni bud med la nyal po byed pa yin no/ /khyim du zhes bya ba ni bram ze dang khyim bdag gi khyim du'o/ /dben pa zhes bya ba ni/ gang na bud med dang / skyes pa dang / ma ning gzhan 'ga' yang med pa'o/ /skyabs yod par zhes bya ba ni ldas bskyabs par te/ rtsig
<p>170b.4</p>pas bskyabs pa dang / rib mas bskyabs pa dang / yol bas bskyabs pa dang / thibs pos bskyabs pa dang / mtshan mos bskyabs par ro/ /'greng na zhes bya ba ni 'dod ma gang gi nang du 'greng na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /sngar nyal po byed par shom pa'i
<p>170b.5</p>khyim du 'dug pa'i ltung byed bstan pa dang / 'dir nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim du 'greng ba'i ltung byed bstan pa de gnyis kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid ni 'dra'o/ /bye brag tu ni/ snga ma ni mngon sum du brnag pas 'dug pa'i yul la rnam par gzhag go/ /'di ni bden pa skyabs yod par
<p>170b.6</p>brnag pas 'greng ba'i yul la rnam par gzhag go/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong 'jigs pa'i dbang dang / gnas gzhan la sems gtod pa ma yin pas khyim pa'i skyes pa dang / bud med gnas gzhan mthong ba'i spyod yul gyi mtha'
<p>170b.7</p>tshun chad kyi gza' tha dad pa ma yin pa nyid dang / mi gzhan med pa nyid kyis spyod du rung ba nyid dang / 'khrig pa spyod pa la zhugs pa'am/ phyogs par shes bzhin du dben pa skyabs yod par brnag pas 'greng zhing spyod par byed pa tshor bya gnyis dang / ltung ba 'byin pa tshor byed
<p>171a</p>
<p>171a.1</p>gnyis kyis tshor ba na nyal bo byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'greng ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ khyim pa'i skyes pa dang / bud med dge slong rang gi gnas las gzhan pa nyid dang / mi gzhan med pa nyid kyis sprad du rung ba nyid ni/ 'khrig
<p>171a.2</p>pa spyod pa la zhugs pa'am/ phyogs pa la 'du shes gtso cher byed pa po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag brgyad kyis dngos bzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong 'jigs pa'i dbang dang / gnas gzhan la yang sems gtod pa ma yin pa nyid dang / khyim pa'i skyes pa nyid dang / bud
<p>171a.3</p>med nyid dang / gnas gzhan dang / mthong ba'i spyod yul gyi mtha' tshun chad kyi gza' tha dad pa nyid dang / mi gzhan med pa nyid kyis sprad du rung ba nyid dang / 'khrig pa spyod pa la zhugs pa'am phyogs pa nyid dang / der 'du shes pa nyid dang / dben pa skyabs yod par brnag pas 'greng
<p>171a.4</p>ba nyid dang / spyod par byed pa tshor bya gnyis dang / ltung ba 'byin pas tshor ba'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /nyal po byed par shom pa'i khyim na 'greng ba'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu gsum pa'o// //gcer bu pa la sbyin pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ 
<p>171a.5</p>sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ko sa la dag tu ljongs rgyu zhing gshegs pa na mnyan yod du byon to/ /mnyan yod na skyed mos tshal zhig na/ yugs sa mo lnga brgya tsam dog pa 'khal zhing 'khod pa de dag gis/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis
<p>171a.6</p>kyis gzugs can brgyan cing gsal ba la sogs pa mthong ngo / /mthong nas kyang 'di lta ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i sems kyis dang por sangs rgyas mthong ba na sems nyams bde ba skyed par byed pa de ltar ni lo bcu gnyis su zhi gnas kyis sems goms par
<p>171a.7</p>byas pa dang / dbul pos gter mthong ba dang / bud med kyis bu thob pa dang / rgyal srid la mngon par dga' ba rgyal srid la dbang bskur ba yang sems nyams bde ba skyed par mi byed pas/ de dag bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la
<p>171b</p>
<p>171b.1</p>mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ mtha' gcig tu 'khod do/ /mtha' gcig tu 'khod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de dag gi bsam pa dang / bag la nyal dang / khams dang rang bzhin thugs su chud nas/ ji nas kyang de dag gis 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i ri'i rtse mo nyi shu mtho ba ye shes
<p>171b.2</p>kyi rdo rjes bcom ste/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu mngon sum du byas par 'gyur ba de ltar chos bstan pa mdzad pas de dag gis rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob bo/ /de dag gis bcom ldan 'das dge slong gi dge 'dun dang bcas pa/ sang bdag cag gi gdugs tshod gsol bar ci
<p>171b.3</p>gnang zhes spyan drangs nas gnang ba dang / kAr ShA pa Na dag khyer te tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo'i gan du song nas smras pa/ btsun pa kun dga' bo bdag cag la snod spyad dang / mi blas dang gnas mal gyi 'byor pa ma mchis kyis/ khyed kyis kyang kAr ShA pa Na 'di dag gis zhal zas sta
<p>171b.4</p>gon bgyid du stsol cig dang / bdag cag mchis te brim par bgyi'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin la/ khyim bdag khyod kyis 'di dag dang bdag nyid kyi kAr ShA pa Na gzhan dag bsres te/ zhal zas bsod pa sta gon gyis la 'dir skur cig
<p>171b.5</p>ces smras so/ /de ltar byas nas rgyal byed kyi tshal du bskur ro/ /tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos/ rigs kyi bu mo de dag la zhal zas sta gon byas kyis tshur sheg la/ sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun la brims shig ces spring ba dang / de dag lhags te smras pa/ btsun pa
<p>171b.6</p>kun dga' bo khyod bdag cag gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen lags kyis/ tshur spyon khyod kyis kyang brim du gsol/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos brim par brtsams pa dang / der gcer bu ma rgan gzhon gnyis shig 'ongs te/ de gnyis kyis khyim bdag mo de dag la zan bslangs pa na/ de
<p>171b.7</p>dag gis smras pa/ zas 'di ni rgyal bu 'di'i yin no/ /gcer bu ma de gnyis kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bslangs pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos ma bsams par brims pa na/ rgan mo la ni khur ba gcig byin/ gzhon nu ma la ni khur ba gnyis sbyin nas/ rgan
<p>172a</p>
<p>172a.1</p>mos smras pa/ gzhon nu ma rgyal bu 'dis khyod don du gnyer gyis/ sta gon gyis shig ces zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag /gcer bu pa dang gcer bu ma kun du rgyu dang / kun du rgyu ma la rang gi lag nas bca' ba dang / bza' ba
<p>172a.2</p>sbyin par byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang gcer bu pa'am/ gcer bu ma kun du rgyu'am/ kun du rgyu
<p>172a.3</p>mo la/ rang gi lag nas bca' ba dang bza' ba sbyin par byed na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ /nyon mongs pa ni ma brtags par spyod pa/ nyes pa ni gcer bu ma la rang gi lag nas zan sbyin pa'o/ /de la yang
<p>172a.4</p>dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni chos 'di pa'o/ /gcer bu pa'am gcer bu ma kun du rgyu'am kun du rgyu mo la zhes bya ba ni/ rtags 'di dang rab tu byung ba 'di med pa la'o/ /rang gi lag nas zhes bya ba ni/ lag pas lag par ro/ /bca' ba dang bza' ba zhes bya ba ni/ bca' ba lnga po dang
<p>172a.5</p>bza' ba lnga po dag go/ /sbyin na zhes bya ba ni bsam mi dgos par ro/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis gzhan mu stegs can gyi rab tu byung ba gcer bu pho yang rung / mo yang rung ba/ rtags 'di dang rab tu
<p>172a.6</p>byung ba 'di med pa/ nye du rab tu byung ba la ltos pa dang / nad pa dang / sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa dang / bral ba nyid ma gtogs pa la rang gi lag nas bca' ba dang / bza' ba zas de la rung ba dag de'i lus sam/ lus dang 'brel par sbyin na/ gcer bu pa la sbyin pa'i ltung byed kyi
<p>172a.7</p>dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ gzhan mu stegs can gyi rab tu byung ba dang / rang gis sbyin pa dang / zas rung ba dag go/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ gzhan mu stegs can gyi rab tu byung ba gcer bu pho yang rung / mo yang rung ba rtags 'di dang
<p>172b</p>
<p>172b.1</p>rab tu byung ba 'di med pa/ nye du rab tu byung ba la ltos pa dang / nad pa dang / sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa dang bral ba nyid ma gtogs pa dang / rang gis sbyin pa dang / zas dang / gnyi ga la rung ba nyid dang / de'i lus sam lus dang 'brel bar sbyin pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag
<p>172b.2</p>ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /gcer bu la sbyin pa'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu bzhi pa'o// //dmag la lta ba'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/ rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /ko sa
<p>172b.3</p>la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis ri brags pa zhig log nas/ der ru pa gcig btang ba dang / bcom zhing rab tu bcom ste phyir 'ongs so/ /ru pa gnyis pa dang gsum pa btang ba dang / de yang bcom zhing rab tu bcom ste phyir 'ongs nas/ ko sa la'i rgyal bo gsal rgyal gyis nga'i
<p>172b.4</p>yul na/ mtshon gyis 'tsho ba gang dag 'khod pa de dag thams cad 'dong bar bya'o zhes dril bsgrags pa byed du bcug ste/ rgyal po'i dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang bcas te 'phags pa dang / drug sde dag gis smras pa/ dga' bo nye dga' gsus po che'i dpung gi tshogs yan
<p>172b.5</p>lag bzhi pa ci 'dra ba bltas 'dong ngo zhes de dag lam kar dong ste 'khod pa dang / ci tsam na ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyi dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dag 'ongs nas/ drug sde dag gis de dag la smras pa/ shes ldan dag gar 'dong / 'phags pa dag ko sa la'i rgyal po
<p>172b.6</p>gsal rgyal gyis ri brags pa zhig log pa de 'bebs su mchi'o/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ bkren pa dag dpung gi tshogs 'di lta bu dag gis/ ri brags pa phebs par 'gyur ram/ khyed kyi glang po che 'di dag ni phag 'dra la/ ri brags pa'i glang po che ni ri bo brtsegs pa 'dra'o/ /
<p>172b.7</p>khyed kyi rta 'di dag ni bong bu 'dra la/ ri brags pa'i rta 'di dag ni glang po che'i phru gu 'dra'o/ /khyed kyi shing rta 'di dag ni/ shing rta zhig pa 'dra la/ ri brags pa'i shing rta dag ni gzhal med khang 'dra'o/ /khyed kyi mi 'di dag ni rtswa mi 'dra la/ ri brags pa'i mi de dag ni gnod sbyin
<p>173a</p>
<p>173a.1</p>gdug pa can 'dra bas khyed cag par 'gro ba yod kyang tshur ldog pa med kyis/ phyir deng la pha ma dag la til gyi chu byin la gzod deng shig /de dag mtha' gcig tu dong ste/ sems khong du chud cing 'khod do/ /ci tsam na ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal 'ongs nas
<p>173a.2</p>des smras pa/ khyed cag ci'i phyir mi 'dong bar mtha' gcig tu dong ste/ sems khong du chud cing 'khod/ de dag gis smras pa/ lha bdag cag rgyal bar ga la 'gyur/ 'di ltar dge sbyong mgo reg ras yug chen glegs pa 'tshal ba 'di dag ni mi mchi dgu mchi'o/ /gang dag
<p>173a.3</p>'phags pa drug sde dag go/ /shes ldan dag de dag ni/ dge sbyong hral po dag yin pas/ de dag gis smras pas khyed la ci gnod deng shig /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis bsams pa/ 'di dag yang dang yang du bdag la tho 'tshams par 'gyur ro snyam du rig nas/ bcom
<p>173a.4</p>ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar mi zhig la phrin gyis bsnyun gsol te/ btsun pa 'phags pa 'di dag dmag chas pa la ltar mchi na/ kye ma bcom ldan 'das kyis gang dag gis 'phags pa dag dmag chas pa la ltar mchi bar mi 'gyur bar dran par bgyi ba cung zhig bca' ba mdzad na legs so
<p>173a.5</p>zhes gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong dmag chas pa la ltar 'gron ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni drug sde/ nyon mongs pa ni ma dul ba/ nyes pa ni dmag chas pa la ltar 'gro ba'o/ /de la yang
<p>173a.6</p>dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni drug sde 'am gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /dmag ces bya ba la/ dmag ni yan lag gcig pa yang yod/ yan lag gnyis pa yang yod/ yan lag gsum pa yang yod/ yan lag bzhi pa yang yod do/ /dmag yan lag gcig pa gang zhe na/ glang po
<p>173a.7</p>che'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag gnyis pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag gsum pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag bzhi pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i
<p>173b</p>
<p>173b.1</p>tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / dpung bu chung gi tshogs so/ /chas pa la zhes bya ba ni g.yul 'gyed pa la mngon par dga' ba la'o/ /ltar 'gro na zhes bya ba ni ltad mo ltar 'gro na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ 
<p>173b.2</p>dge slong rgyal po dang / btsun mo dang / gzhon nu dang / zhang blon dang / khrom gyi ru sna dang / grong rdal gyi mi dang / ljongs kyi mis bkug pa dang / bar chad byung ba'i dbang nyid ma gtogs pas g.yul la mngon par dga' ba'i dmag la lta ba'i don nyid kyis 'phags pa'i nyen kor gyi mtha'
<p>173b.3</p>las 'das te mthong na/ dmag la lta ba'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni g.yul la mngon par dga' ba'i dmag la lta ba'i don nyid kyis/ 'phags pa'i nyen kor gyi mtha' las 'das te mthong ba'o/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ 
<p>173b.4</p>dge slong rgyal po dang / btsun mo dang / gzhon nu dang / zhang blon dang / khrom gyi ru sna dang / grong rdal gyi mi dang / ljongs kyi mis bkug pa dang / bar chad 'byung ba'i dbang nyid ma gtogs pa dang / g.yul las mngon par dga' ba'i dmag nyid dang / lta ba'i don nyid dang 'phags
<p>173b.5</p>pa'i nyen kor gyi mtha' las 'das pa dang mthong ba'o/ /'di dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs skrun smad do/ /dmag la lta ba'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu lnga pa'o// //so sor thar pa'i mdo'i gzhung 'grel/ bam po bcu gsum pa/ dmag gi nang na gnas pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ 
<p>173b.6</p>sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /ri brags pa de de lta shAn yang ma phebs nas/ rgyal pos de nyid du phru ma btab ste 'dug pa dang / blon po rnams kyis smras pa/ lha khyim bdag mgon med zas
<p>173b.7</p>sbyin ni bsod nams kyi rnam par smin pa can dbang che bar grags pa lags pas/ gal te de mchis par gyur na de'i mthus ri brags pa 'di phebs par 'gyur ba gang lags pa de lta bu gnas mchis par 'gyur gda'o/ /rgyal pos khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin la khyim bdag mthong
<p>174a</p>
<p>174a.1</p>bar 'dod do zhes yi ge spring ba dang / khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin der 'ongs so/ /de lta na yang ri brags pa de ma phebs nas/ ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis/ khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin la smras pa/ khyim bdag khye'u dag mi dran nam/ lha
<p>174a.2</p>khye'u dag mi dran te/ 'di ltar 'phags pa dag mthong bar 'tshal lo/ /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis/ dge 'dun la/ 'phags pa dag mthong bar 'tshal lo zhes yi ge spring ba dang / dge skos kyis dge 'dun gyi dbus su yi ge bklags te/ gang der 'gro bar spro ba des
<p>174a.3</p>tshul shing long shig ces/ tshul shing brims pa dang / dge slong gnas brtan gnas brtan dag gis smras pa/ kho bo cag ni rgan po sbyor mi bzod pa dag yin pas der 'gro mi nus so/ /dge slong gsar bu gsar bu dag gis smras pa/ der chos bstan par bya dgos na/ bdag
<p>174a.4</p>cag ni thos pa nyung ba yin pas chos bstan par mi nus na/ der chu brim par bya'am ci/ bdag cag kyang der 'gro mi nus so/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ dga' bo nye dga' ji srid du bcom ldan 'das bzhugs shing / bdag cag gson pa de srid du bstan pa gnas la/ bcom
<p>174a.5</p>ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'das shing / bdag cag dus la bab pa na/ bstan pa nub par brjod par bya ste/ ji srid du bdag cag gson pa de srid du bstan pa la gces pa bskyed par byas/ tshul shing blang ngo zhes de dag gis tshul shing blangs te der dong nas rgyal po la chos
<p>174a.6</p>bstan pas/ rgyal po mngon par dad par byas so/ /btsun mo dang / gzhon nu dag dang / zhang blon dang / khrom gyi ru sna dag la yang chos bstan pas skye bo phal po che'i tshogs mngon par dad par byas so/ /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis blon po rnams la smras pa/ ri brags
<p>174a.7</p>pa bskor du dong ngo zhes de dag 'phags pa dang / drug sde dag gis smras pa/ dga' bo nye dga' bdag cag gis yun ji srid du gzhan gyi spyod lam gyis gnas par bya'am/ /gsus po che'i dmag ci 'dra ba ltar 'dong ngo zhes de dag lam kar dong ste 'khod pa dang / ci tsam na dpung gi tshogs
<p>174b</p>
<p>174b.1</p>yan lag bzhi pa 'ongs nas/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag shul phye shig /ci bya/ dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa mchi'o/ /bkren pa dag 'di 'dra ba dag glang po che yin nam/ phag 'dra'o zhes de dag gis de dag gi mche ba dag nas bzung ste/ mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /'di 'dra ba dag
<p>174b.2</p>rta yin nam bong bu 'dra'o zhes de dag gis de dag gi mjug ma dag nas bzung ste mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /'di 'dra ba dag shing rta yin nam/ shing rta zhig pa dag 'dra'o zhes de dag gis de dag gi srog shing dag nas bzung ste mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /'di 'dra ba dag mi yin nam rtswa mi dag
<p>174b.3</p>'dra'o zhes de dag gis de dag gi gnya' bdag nas bzung ste/ mtha' gcig tu bor nas de dag sems khong du chud nas 'khod do/ /ji tsam na ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal 'ongs nas des smras pa/ shes ldan dag ci'i phyir khyed cag mi dong bar sems khong du chud cing 'khod/ lha
<p>174b.4</p>bdag cag rgyal bar ga la 'gyur/ 'di ltar dge sbyong mgo reg ras yug chen glegs pa/ 'tshal ba 'di dag mi mchi dgu mchi'o/ /gang dag /'phags pa drug sde dag go/ /shes ldan dag /de dag ni dge sbyong hral po dag yin pas de dag gis smras pas khyed la ci gnod deng shig /ko
<p>174b.5</p>sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis bsams pa/ 'di dag yang dang yang du bdag la tho 'tshams par 'gyur ro snyam du rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar mi zhig la phrin gyis bsnyun gsol nas/ btsun pa 'phags pa 'di dag dmag chas pa la ltar mchis nas/ shin tu yun
<p>174b.6</p>ring por dmag gi nang na gnas na/ kye bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ gang gis 'phags pa dag dmag chas pa la ltar mchis nas/ shin tu yun ring por dmag gi nang na gnas par mi 'gyur bar/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'phags pa rnams la dran par
<p>174b.7</p>bgyi ba cung zhig bca' ba mdzad na legs so zhes gsol lo/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ dge slong la dmag chas pa la ltar 'gro ba de lta bu'i rkyen zhig byung na/ dge slong des dmag de'i nang du zhag gnyis tshun chad gnas par bya'o/ /de las lhag par
<p>175a</p>
<p>175a.1</p>gnas na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni drug sde/ nyon mongs pa ni ma dul ba/ nyes pa ni shin tu yun ring por dmag gi nang na gnas pa'o/ /de la dge slong gang la zhes bya ba ni drug sde 'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu
<p>175a.2</p>gang yin pa'o/ /dmag ces bya ba la/ dmag ni yan lag gcig pa yang yod/ yan lag gnyis pa yang yod/ yan lag gsum pa yang yod/ yan lag bzhi pa yang yod do/ /dmag yan lag gcig pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag gnyis pa
<p>175a.3</p>gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag gsum pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag bzhi pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / 
<p>175a.4</p>dpung bu chung gi tshogs so/ /chas pa la zhes bya ba ni g.yul 'gyed par mngon par dga' ba la'o/ /ltar 'gro ba zhes bya ba ni rgyu gang gis so/ /de lta bu'i rkyen zhig byung na zhes bya ba ni/ rgyal po dang / btsun mo dang / gzhon nu dang / zhang blon dang / khrom gyi ru sna dang / grong rdal
<p>175a.5</p>gyi mi dang / ljongs kyi mis bkug na'o/ /dge slong des zhes bya ba ni/ dge slong gang yin pa des so/ /dmag de'i nang du zhes bya ba ni dmag chas pa de'i nang du'o/ /zhag gnyis tshun chad gnas par bya'o zhes bya ba ni/ zhag gnyis kyi mtha' tshun chad gnas par bya ba'o/ /de las
<p>175a.6</p>lhag par gnas na zhes bya ba ni/ de las 'das par gnas na'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong rgyal po dang / btsun mo dang / gzhon nu dang / zhang blon dang / khrom gyi ru sna dang / grong rdal gyi mi dang / 
<p>175a.7</p>ljongs kyi mis bkug pa dang / bar chad kyi dbang nyid byung na g.yul la mngon par dga' ba dmag de'i nang du nyin mtshan gnyis las lhag par nyin mtshan gsum pa'i skya rengs dang po shar bar gnas sam/ rgyal po la sogs pas bkug pa dang / bar chad kyi dbang de dag med
<p>175b</p>
<p>175b.1</p>par lta ba'i don nyid kyis g.yul la mngon par dga' ba'i dmag de'i nang du nyin mtshan gsum pa'i snga ma nyin mtshan gcig dang / gnyis kyi mthar gnas na yang dmag gi nang na gnas pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ rgyal po la sogs pas bkug pa dang / 
<p>175b.2</p>bar chad kyi dbang de dag yod na g.yul la mngon par dga' ba'i dmag gi nang du/ skya rengs gsum pa shar ba dang / de dag med par zhag gcig dang gnyis kyi skya rengs shar ba'o/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong rgyal po la sogs pas bkug
<p>175b.3</p>pa dang / bar chad kyi dbang gis dgos pa yod pa dang / g.yul la mngon par dga' ba'i dmag nyid dang der skya rengs gsum shar ba dang / dgos pa de dag med par der zhag gcig gi skya rengs shar ba dang / dgos pa de dag med par der zhag gnyis pa'i skya rengs shar ba'o/ /
<p>175b.4</p>de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /dmag gi nang na gnas pa'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu drug pa'o// //dpung gi yan lag nyams su myong bar byed pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal/ mgon med
<p>175b.5</p>zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /ri brags pa de de lta na yang ma phebs nas/ ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis/ khyim pa dag mgon med zas sbyin la smras pa/ khyim bdag khye'u dag mi dran nam/ lha khye'u dag ni mi dran te/ 'di ltar 'phags pa dag mthong bar 'tshal
<p>175b.6</p>lo/ /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis/ dge 'dun la 'phags pa dag mthong bar 'tshal lo zhes yi ge spring ba dang / dge skos kyis dge 'dun gyi nang du yi ge bklags te/ gang der 'gro bar spro ba des tshul shing long shig ces tshul shing brims pa dang / dge slong gnas brtan
<p>175b.7</p>gnas brtan dag gis smras pa/ kho bo cag ni rgan po sbyor mi bzod pa dag yin pas der 'gro mi nus so/ /dge slong gsar bu gsar bu dag gis smras pa/ der chos bstan par bya dgos na bdag cag ni thos pa nyung ba yin pas chos ston par mi nus na/ der chu brim par bya'am ci/ 
<p>176a</p>
<p>176a.1</p>bdag cag kyang der 'gro mi nus so/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ dga' bo nye dga' ji srid du bcom ldan 'das bzhugs shing / bdag cag gson pa de srid du bstan pa gnas la/ bcom ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'das shing / bdag cag dus la bab na bstan
<p>176a.2</p>pa nub par brjod par bya ste/ ji srid du bdag cag gson pa de srid du bstan pa la gces pa brjod par byas/ tshul shing blang ngo zhes de dag gis tshul shing blangs te/ der dong nas rgyal po la chos bstan pas rgyal po mngon par dad par byas so/ /btsun mo dag dang / gzhon nu dag dang / zhang
<p>176a.3</p>blon dag dang / khrom gyi ru sna dag la yang chos bstan pas skye bo phal po che'i tshogs mngon par dad par byas so/ /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis blon po rnams la smras pa/ ded la g.yul shoms shig ri brags pa bskor bar bya'o/ /de dag gis g.yul bsham par brtsams pa dang / 
<p>176a.4</p>drug sde dag gis smras pa/ dga' bo nye dga' bdag cag gis yun ji srid du gzhan gyi spyod lam gyis gnas par bya/ rang gi spyod lam gyis gnas par byas/ gsus po che'i rgyal mtshan gyi mchog dang / dpung gi mchog dang g.yul bkod cing bshams pa'i dmag la lta ba nyams su myong bar
<p>176a.5</p>byas 'dong ngo zhes de dag g.yul shom pa'i nang du dong ste dris pa/ shes ldan dag ci byed/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag bkod pa shom mo/ /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ bkren pa dag glang po che bcos ma 'di lta bu dag phyogs 'dir 'jog gam/ 'di sol cig ces de dag gis de dag
<p>176a.6</p>gi mche ba dag nas bzung ste mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /rta theng po 'di lta bu dag phyogs 'dir 'jog gam/ 'di sol cig ces de dag gis mjug ma dag nas bzung ste mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /shing rta zhig pa 'di lta bu dag phyogs 'dir 'jog gam/ 'di sol cig ces de dag
<p>176a.7</p>gis de dag gi srog shing dag nas bzung ste mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /mi zhar ba 'di lta bu dag phyogs 'dir 'jog gam/ 'di sol cig ces de dag gis de dag gi gnya' ba dag nas bzung ste/ mtha' gcig tu bor ro/ /drug sde dag gi mdun logs su ri brags pa dang / ha cang thag mi
<p>176b</p>
<p>176b.1</p>ring bar 'khod de blag cor gyis sgra phyung ba dang / de dag gis bsams pa/ ri brags pa dag rdzong nas rlugs te phyung ngo snyam du rig nas/ skrag cing sdangs te bros par brtsams pa dang / drug sde dag myur ba myur bar dong ste/ khrom gyi ru sna'i mdun du 'khod nas smras pa/ shes ldan dag ci'i
<p>176b.2</p>phyir bros/ de dag gis smras pa/ 'phags pa dag ri brags pa dag rdzong nas rlugs te phyung ngo / /drug sde dag gis smras pa/ bkren pa dag de ni kho bo cag gis ku re cung zhig byas pa yin te/ gal te ri brags pa dag gis khyed cag de ltar byed ngas par shes shing rig par gyur na/ nang par
<p>176b.3</p>snga ba kho nar yang khyed cag gnyis ka gnya' ba dag nas btags te ri brags su khrid par 'gyur gyis/ ma 'jigs par phyir log shig /de dag phyogs gcig tu dong ste/ sems khong du chud cing 'khod do/ /ji tsam na ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal 'ongs nas des smras pa/ 
<p>176b.4</p>shes ldan dag khyed kyis da dung yang g.yul gyi bkod pa ma bshams sam/ de dag gis smras pa/ lha bdag cag rgyal bar ga la 'gyur 'di lta ste/ dge sbyong ras yug chen glegs pa 'tshal ba 'di dag mchis nas bdag cag la tho 'tshams shing / mi mchi dgu mchi'o/ /gang
<p>176b.5</p>dag /'phags pa drug sde dag go/ /shes ldan dag de dag ni dge sbyong hral po dag yin pas/ de dag gis smras pas khyed la ci gnod/ deng la g.yul gyi bkod pa shoms shig /ko sa la'i rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis bsams pa/ 'di dag yang dang yang du bdag la tho 'tshams
<p>176b.6</p>par 'gyur ro snyam du rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar mi zhig la phrin gyis bsnyun gsol te/ btsun pa 'phags pa 'di dag /shin du yun ring por dmag gi nang na gnas pa'i tshe yang bshams pa 'khrug tu mi mchi zhing / /rgyal mtshan gyi mchog dang / dpung gi
<p>176b.7</p>mchog dang / g.yul bshams pa'i dmag la lta ba nyams su myong bar bgyid par mi 'gyur bar/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'phags pa rnams la dran par bgyi ba cung zhig bca' ba mdzad na legs so zhes gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ dge slong
<p>177a</p>
<p>177a.1</p>zhag gnyis dmag gi nang na gnas pa'i tshe yang gal te bshams pa 'khrug tu 'gro'am/ rgyal mtshan gyi mchog gam/ dpung gi mchog gam/ g.yul bshams pa'i dmag la lta ba nyams su myong bar byed na ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni
<p>177a.2</p>mnyan yod/ gang zag ni drug sde/ nyon mongs pa ni ma dul ba/ nyes pa ni zhag gnyis dmag de'i nang na gnas pa'i tshe yang dpung gi yan lag nyams su myong bar byed pa'o/ /de la dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni drug sde'am gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /zhag gnyis zhes bya ba ni
<p>177a.3</p>zhag gnyis tshun chad do/ /dmag ces bya ba la/ dmag ni yan lag gcig pa yang yod/ yan lag gnyis pa yang yod/ yan lag gsum pa yang yod/ dmag yan lag bzhi pa yang yod do/ /dmag yan lag gcig pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag
<p>177a.4</p>gnyis pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag gsum pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs so/ /dmag yan lag bzhi pa gang zhe na/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / 
<p>177a.5</p>dpung bu chung gi tshogs so/ /de'i nang na gnas pa'i tshe yang zhes bya ba ni 'dug pa'i tshe yang ngo / /gal te bshams pa 'khrug tu 'gro'am zhes bya ba ni g.yul la chas pa 'khrug tu 'gro ba'o/ /rgyal mtshan gyi mchog ces bya ba ni/ rgyal mtshan rnam pa bzhi ste/ khyu mchog gi rgyal
<p>177a.6</p>mtshan dang / chu srin gyi rgyal mtshan dang / seng ge'i rgyal mtshan dang / klu'i rgyal mtshan no/ /dpung gi mchog ces bya ba ni/ dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa ste/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / dpung bu chung gi tshogs so/ /g.yul
<p>177a.7</p>bshams pa'i dmag la lta ba nyams su myong bar byed na zhes bya ba la/ bshams pa ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ 'bru'i kha lta bu dang / shing rta'i dbyibs lta bu dang / zla gam gyi rnam pa lta bu dang / nam mkha' lding gi 'dab ma lta bu'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /de la 'dir
<p>177b</p>
<p>177b.1</p>dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong bar chad kyi dbang gis 'gro ba ma yin pas dpung gi yan lag bsdus pa'am/ so so ba sta gon byas pa rnams kyi dngos po reg pa dang / bshams pa dkrugs pa dang / lta ba'i phyir 'phags shing nyen kor gyi mtha' las 'das te/ 
<p>177b.2</p>mthong ba lta bu nyams su myong na/ dpung gi yan lag nyams su myong bar byed pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ dge slong bar chad kyi dbang gis 'gro ba ma yin pa la dpung gi yan lag bsdus pa'am/ so so ba sta gon byas pa rnams kyi dngos po byed pa
<p>177b.3</p>po nyid yin no/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ dge slong bar chad kyi dbang gis 'gro ba ma yin pa dang / dpung gi yan lag bzhi po rnams dang / bsdus pa'am/ so so ba gang yang rung ba dang / sta gon byas pa rnams kyi dngos po reg pa dang / 
<p>177b.4</p>bshams pa dkrugs pa dang / lta ba'i phyir 'phags shing nyen kor gyi mtha' las 'das te mthong ba lta bu gang yang rung ba dang de dag nyams su myong ba'o/ /de dag las yan lag ma tshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /dpung gi yan lag nyams su myong bar byed pa'i ltung byed
<p>177b.5</p>de bzhi bcu bdun pa'o// //rdeg pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /gang gi tshe tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen pos nye ba 'khor la sogs pa sar
<p>177b.6</p>pa skyes phran gzhon nu bcu bdun sde'i tshogs dag rab tu phyung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs par byas pa de'i tshe na/ de dag drug sde dag la sten par byed/ bsnyen par byed/ bsnyen bkur byed do/ /de nas 'char kas smras pa/ bcu bdun sde dag tshur shog /'di dang 'di gyis shig /
<p>177b.7</p>de dag gis smras pa/ ci khyod kho bo cag gi slob dpon yin nam mkhan po yin mi byed do/ /des glen pa dag khyod las ci zhig byed ces de dag las gcig brdegs pa dang / de dag thams cad kyis bdag cag brdegs so/ /bdag cag brdegs so zhes phyi gan du bsgyel te ngu bar
<p>178a</p>
<p>178a.1</p>brtsams so/ /dge slong rnams kyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa 'char ka ci'i phyir gzhon nu rnams la rdeg par byed/ 'char kas smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa dag kho bos gcig brdegs pa dang / thams cad sa la bsgyel te ngu'o/ /dge slong rnams kyis bcu
<p>178a.2</p>bdun sde dag la smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa dag khyed cag las gcig brdegs na/ ci'i phyir thams cad sa la bsgyel te ngu / de dag gis smras pa/ gal te ma ngus na thams cad la rdeg par 'gyur ro zhes zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag khros 'khrugs
<p>178a.3</p>rngam par gyur te/ yid ma rangs nas/ dge slong la rdeg par byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang
<p>178a.4</p>khros 'khrugs rngam par gyur te/ yid ma rangs nas/ dge slong la brdegs te ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni 'char ka /nyon mongs pa ni zhe sdang gi kun du sbyor ba/ nyes pa ni dge slong la rdeg pa'o/ /de la yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni 'char
<p>178a.5</p>ka'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /khros 'khrugs rngam par gyur te yid ma rangs nas zhes bya ba ni/ khros shing khro ba'i zil gyis non nas so/ /dge slong la zhes bya ba ni chos 'di pa la'o/ /brdegs na zhes bya ba ni rdeg par byed pa'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /
<p>178a.6</p>de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis rnyog pa can gyi sems nyid kyis dge slong pha rol la lus sam des 'phangs pa'am/ de dang 'brel pa dag gang yang rung ba tha na rkang pa'i mthe bo'am/ yungs kar ram/ rtswa dag gis brdegs na reg pa tsam gyis rdeg
<p>178a.7</p>spyad re re la rdeg pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni/ pha rol po brdeg par bya ba dge slong nyid dang / rdeg spyad gang yang rung ba ji snyed pa'o/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos gzhi'i ltung bar 'gyur te/ rnyog pa can gyi sems nyid dang / pha rol po brdeg par
<p>178b</p>
<p>178b.1</p>bya ba dge slong nyid dang / rdeg pa lus sam des 'phangs pa'am/ de dang 'brel pa gang yang rung ba dang / rdeg spyad tha na rkang pa'i mthe bo'am/ yungs kar ram/ rtswa bas chung ba gang yang rung ba dang / tha na lus la reg pa'o/ /de dag las yan lag mtshang na ci rigs par na smad do/ /rdeg
<p>178b.2</p>pa'i ltung byed de bzhi bcu brgyad pa'o// //gzas pa'i ltung byed kyi gleng gzhi ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/ rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs so/ /gang gi tshe tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen pos/ nye ba 'khor la
<p>178b.3</p>sogs pa sar pa skyes phran gzhon nu bcu bdun sde'i tshogs dag rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs par byas pa de'i tshe na/ de dag drug sde dag la sten par byed/ bsnyen par byed/ bsnyen bkur byed do/ /de nas 'char kas smras pa/ bcu bdun sde dag tshur shog /'di dang 'di gyis shig /
<p>178b.4</p>de dag gis smras pa/ ci khyed kho bo cag gi slob dpon yin nam mkhan po yin mi byed do/ /des glen pa dag khyed ci zhig byed ces de dag las gcig la rdeg par gzas pa dang / de dag thams cad kyis bdag cag la rdeg par gzas so/ /bdag cag la rdeg par gzas so zhes phyi gan du
<p>178b.5</p>bsgyel te ngu bar brtsams so/ /dge slong rnams kyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa 'char ka ci'i phyir gzhon nu dag la rdeg par gzas/ 'char kas smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa kho bos gcig la rdeg par gzas pa dang / thams cad sa la 'gyel te ngu'o/ /dge slong rnams kyis bcu bdun sde
<p>178b.6</p>dag la smras pa/ khyed cag las gcig la rdeg par gzes pa na/ ci'i phyir thams cad sa la bsgyel te ngu / de dag gis smras pa/ gal te ma ngus na gang la cis rdeg gtol med do zhes zer nas/ dge slong don nyung ngu dag ci'i phyir dge slong dag khros 'khrugs rngam par gyur te yid ma
<p>178b.7</p>rangs nas/ dge slong la rdeg par gzas par byed ces smod par byed/ phyar ka gtong bar byed/ kha zer bar byed pa'i skabs de/ dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis snga ma bzhin du/ yang dge slong gang khros 'khrugs rngam par gyur te/ 
<p>179a</p>
<p>179a.1</p>yid ma rangs nas/ dge slong la rdeg par gzas na/ tha na thal mos kyang rung ste/ ltung byed do zhes bca' ba mdzad de/ yul ni mnyan yod/ gang zag ni 'char ka /nyon mongs pa ni zhe sdang gi kun du sbyor ba/ nyes pa ni dge slong la rdeg par gzas pa'o/ /de la
<p>179a.2</p>yang dge slong gang zhes bya ba ni 'char ka'am/ gzhan yang de lta bu gang yin pa'o/ /khros 'khrugs rngam par gyur te yid ma rangs nas zhes bya ba ni/ khros shing khro ba'i zil gyis non nas so/ /dge slong la zhes bya ba ni chos 'di pa la'o/ /rdeg par gzas na zhes bya ba ni/ brdeg par bshams
<p>179a.3</p>na'o/ /tha na thal mos kyang rung ste zhes bya ba ni/ tha na thal lcag kyang gzas kyang rung ste'o/ /ltung byed do zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /sngar rdeg pa'i ltung byed bstan pa dang / 'dir gzas pa'i ltung byed bstan pa de gnyis kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid ni 'dra'o bye brag tu na/ snga ma ni brdegs pa'i yul la
<p>179a.4</p>rnam par gzhag go/ /'di ni rdeg par gzas pa'i yul la rnam par gzhag go/ /de la 'dir dngos gzhi'i ltung ba rnam par gzhag pa ni/ dge slong gis rnyog pa can gyi sems nyid kyis dge slong pha rol la lus sam/ des 'phangs pa'am/ de dang 'brel ba dag gang yang rung ba tha na rkang pa'i
<p>179a.5</p>mthe bo'am/ yungs kar ram/ rtswa dag gis rdeg par gzas na/ gzas pa tsam gyis rdzas re re la gzas pa'i ltung byed kyi dngos gzhir 'gyur ro/ /'di'i byed pa po ni pha rol po la rdeg par gzas pa dge slong nyid dang / gzo ba'i rdzas gang yang rung ba ji snyed pa'o/ /'di la yan lag lngas dngos
